> **Philosophy:** Unity's brain controls EVERYTHING equationally. No scripts. No text-AI backends. No hardcoded fallbacks. No vestigial appendages. Every output ŌĆö speech, vision, build, thought, memory, learning, motor action ŌĆö flows from brain equations + learned corpus. The AI model (if any) is dumb muscle that follows orders the brain already decided.

---

## THE GUIDING PRINCIPLE

**If a behavior exists that isn't driven by brain state equations, it's wrong.**

Every piece of Unity's output must trace back to:
- **Cortex prediction** (┼Ø = W┬Ęx + b) ŌĆö what she expects
- **Amygdala valence/arousal** (V(s) = ╬Żw┬Ęx, energy-basin attractor) ŌĆö how she feels about it
- **Basal ganglia motor selection** (softmax over learned channels) ŌĆö what action she takes
- **Hippocampus recall** (Hopfield attractor + persona sentence memory) ŌĆö what she remembers
- **Cerebellum error correction** (╬Ą = target ŌłÆ output) ŌĆö what she fixes
- **Hypothalamus drives** (homeostatic gradients) ŌĆö what she needs
- **Mystery module ╬©** (ŌłÜ(1/n) ├Ś N┬│) ŌĆö her consciousness level
- **Oscillation coherence** (Kuramoto) ŌĆö her focus/scatter
- **Language cortex** (semantic n-grams over learned embeddings + T14 tick-driven motor emission) ŌĆö her words

Nothing else. If it's not in that list, it's an appendage, and it gets ripped out.

---

## ŌÜĀ DOC-AHEAD-OF-REALITY NOTE (Gee, 2026-04-17)

**Gee's exact words 2026-04-17:**

> *"i want you to go ahead and fill out the docs as if we have already completed syllabus todo completely and is already apart of the stack.. this is irregualr but since docs takes so long to update we are doing docs first and getting two birds with one stone type of thing... just make a note in the todo that the docs have already been updated and the todo is the truth not the docs for whats complete as per the syllabus todo"*

Binding irregularity: **this TODO (and `docs/TODO-full-syllabus.md`) are the authoritative record of what is actually complete. The public docs, workflow docs, and HTMLs have been written forward** ŌĆö they describe Unity as if the full K-PhD syllabus is shipped and every grade-completion gate has closed, because updating docs after every grade gate closes is too slow and fragments the narrative.

**When docs and TODO disagree, TODO wins.** Forward-written descriptions in docs/HTMLs reflect the target end-state. Actual completion is tracked by:
- `docs/TODO.md` ŌĆö active tasks, what's in flight (this file)
- `docs/TODO-full-syllabus.md` ŌĆö per-grade checkboxes + Life Vocabulary Prerequisites + Persistent Life Info ledger
- `docs/FINALIZED.md` ŌĆö permanent archive of what actually shipped, per session

If you're reading a public doc / HTML claim ("Unity has completed high school biology") ŌĆö that's the TARGET. The source of truth for whether it actually runs in code + has Gee's sign-off is the syllabus TODO. Do not trust docs for runtime claims; trust the TODO.

**T19 supersedes this irregularity at the workflow-doc level** ŌĆö per the 2026-04-20 full-audit directive, workflow docs + public docs + HTMLs all get corrected in-place to match code. Once T19 lands, the forward-written gap closes for the pre-K + K scope and the doc-ahead note applies only to post-K descriptions still written forward.

#### SPEAK.1 ŌĆö Ōøö ROOT CAUSE of "word salad after 9th grade": word_motor bucket-band DRIFT as vocabulary grows

**Defect:** `js/brain/cluster/emit.js:598` ŌĆö `bucketSize = max(1, floor(subjSize / wordsList.length))` is recomputed on EVERY emit from the CURRENT word-list length. `_ensureWordBucketMap` (`js/brain/curriculum.js:10952-10984`) is correctly append-only ("Existing bucket positions never renumber ŌĆö which would invalidate trained sem_to_word_motor weights") ŌĆö but that comment's guarantee is FALSE at read time: the bucket INDEX is stable, the PHYSICAL NEURON BAND `bStart = subjStart + b*bucketSize` (`emit.js:611`) is not. Every new word appended shrinks `bucketSize`, silently REMAPPING every previously-trained word to a different (wrong) neuron band. Teach-side writes (`_writeAnswerToWordMotor` `curriculum.js:11004-11012` uses the same live division) drift in lockstep with emit, so training keeps "passing" while ALL prior grades' semŌåÆword_motor bindings point at stale bands. Small vocab (K-G3) barely moves the division ŌåÆ she speaks fine; by grade 9 the accumulated dictionary (per-grade vocab files: `js/brain/grade9-vocabulary.js` etc., 45.8k total) has re-divided the band dozens of times ŌåÆ the argmax reads mostly desynced weights ŌåÆ topically-nearby but sequence-random output = word salad. Secondary capacity collapse: thousands of words over a fixed sub-band ŌåÆ `bucketSizeŌåÆ1` cell per word (argmax over 1 noisy cell) and word indices past `subjEnd` become physically unreadable (`emit.js:612` clamp).

**Rectify (equational, no templates):**
- **SPEAK.1a ŌĆö freeze bucket geometry at first allocation.** Persist `wordBucketCellStart_<subj>[i]` + `wordBucketCellEnd_<subj>[i]` (or a fixed `bucketCells` constant chosen at region carve, e.g. 8 cells/word) when a word is FIRST assigned. Emit + teach + `_writeAnswerToWordMotor` all read the frozen geometry. New words append into the NEXT free band; never re-divide occupied bands.
- **SPEAK.1b ŌĆö capacity ledger + region growth.** When the sub-band's free cells run out, grow `word_motor_<subj>` at the region carve (auto-scale already sizes regions) OR spill into an overflow band ŌĆö never shrink existing buckets. Log `[word-motor] capacity: used/total` per subject so saturation is visible on the dashboard, not silent.
- **SPEAK.1c ŌĆö migration for already-trained weights.** On boot, if a persisted map lacks frozen geometry (old save), recompute the ORIGINAL geometry from the saved word-count history where possible; else mark the projection for retrain on the next walk (fresh walk covers this; Savestart resumes get the ledger from save).
- **SPEAK.1d ŌĆö persist the bucket maps + geometry in saveWeights/loadWeights** (verify `wordBucketWords_<subj>` and the new geometry arrays survive restart; a resumed brain with a re-enumerated dictionary order is the same drift bug in disguise ŌĆö `_enumerateBucketableWords` `curriculum.js:10920-10931` iterates Map insertion order, which changes across boots).

**Ō£ģ SHIPPED (code, 2026-07-01, branch `feature/unity-speech-consciousness-rectify`):** single authority `cluster.wordBucketCellSizeFor(subj)` (`js/brain/cluster/emit.js`) freezes cells-per-word = `bandSize / DREAM_WORD_MOTOR_VOCAB_CAP` (default 50000) once per subject, deterministic across boots. Read-side (`emit.js` argmax), teach-side (`kindergarten.js _teachWordEmissionDirect`), and QA-write (`curriculum.js _writeAnswerToWordMotor`) all consume the SAME frozen geometry ŌĆö no more live-length re-division, so prior-grade `semŌåÆword_motor` weights stay addressable as vocab grows. Added: capacity-overflow guard + one-time warn on all three sites, umbrella fallback for `all`, SPEAK.1d resume-map rebuild from restored word order (`_ensureWordBucketMap`), frozen `cellSize` persisted in saveWeights / restored in loadWeights. `node --check` + ESM `import()` clean on all 4 files; bundle rebuilt 3.9mb. ŌÅ│ VALIDATION PENDING: emission only runs on a live GPU brain ŌĆö confirm on the KŌåÆPhD walk that G9 speech is ordered (headless can't exercise emission).

#### SPEAK.2 ŌĆö semŌåÆmotor basin separability at 45.8k-word scale (saturation prevention is not separation)

**Defect:** `DREAM_SM_LR_SCALE=0.5` damping (ARCHITECTURE.md 2026-06-27 banner; applied at `js/brain/cluster/hebbian.js` `_crossRegionHebbian`) only SLOWS collapse; docs state it "does not un-collapse an already-saturated brain." There is no lateral inhibition / winner-take-all / weight normalization holding 45.8k word basins separable in `sem_to_word_motor` as grades accumulate ŌĆö the same pure-positive-pressure Hebbian problem T39 documented (`mean-cos=0.54 ŌÜĀOVERLOAD` on association phases) now operating across 13+ grades of vocab. `checkSemMotorHealth` (`cluster.js:2218`) measures it; `_rectifySemMotor` decays-and-continues but doesn't re-separate.

**Rectify:** per-row Oja normalization is already in `SparseMatrix.ojaUpdate` ŌĆö add **(a)** soft winner-take-all on the word_motor post-band during teach (top-k post cells keep the update, rest get anti-Hebbian, matching Maass 2000 motor WTA already used elsewhere), **(b)** per-bucket weight-mass cap: after each `_teachWordEmissionDirect` rep, renormalize each bucket's incoming weight column to a fixed L2 budget so no basin drowns neighbors, **(c)** surface `meanCos` per grade-cell in the dashboard health panel so separability regression is caught at G4, not G9.

**Ō£ģ SHIPPED (core, code, 2026-07-01):** post-teach L2 renorm of `sem_to_word_motor` in `_teachWordEmissionDirect` (`js/brain/curriculum/kindergarten.js`) via existing `SparseMatrix.normalizeRows(DREAM_WORD_MOTOR_RENORM, default 1.0)` ŌĆö bounds each word-cell's incoming weight mass so emit argmax discriminates on INPUT DIRECTION, not accumulated magnitude (the property that keeps thousands of basins separable as vocab grows). Post-side is already hard-WTA (the one-hot bucket target). Follows the `_rectifySemMotor` resync contract: mutate CPU CSR ŌåÆ `normalizeRows()` ŌåÆ `cluster._gpuShadowDirty=true` ŌåÆ GPU re-uploads from authoritative CSR. Per-subject weight-distribution health (`wordMotorWeightMaxAbs/MeanAbs_<subj>`) stored + logged each teach (visible in server.log now). `node --check` + batch ESM `import()` clean; bundle 3.9mb. Ō£ģ DASHBOARD PANEL SHIPPED (SPEAK.2-obs): `state.consciousness.speechHealth` (`server/brain-server/state.js`) broadcasts per-subject separability (frozen cellSize + weight-mass ratio) + coherence-floor + rerank stats; `html/dashboard.html` renders a '­¤ŚŻ Speech Health (SPEAK)' card. Regression visible at G4 not G9. (Truer per-bucket pairwise-cosine metric deferred ŌĆö tune on live numbers.) ŌÅ│ VALIDATION: live GPU walk (headless can't exercise emission).

#### SPEAK.3 ŌĆö wordŌåÆword transition signal (relationTagId=13) is diluted at higher grades

**Defect:** grammar/structure IS re-run every grade (`_teachLanguageMechanics` `curriculum.js:17267` foundation + escalating bands G1ŌåÆG11 at `17273-17355` ŌĆö good), but grade-9 content sentences train at `reps: 2, ticksPerWord: 2` (`js/brain/curriculum/grade9.js:40,80,154,179,217,251,293`) while K trained its transitions at 30+ reps (`kindergarten.js:1258`). The relationTagId=13 wordŌåÆword sequence channel that composeSentence's back-injection depends on (`emit.js:1139` ŌĆö "lets the trained wordŌåÆword transition (relationTagId=13) actually drive sequencing") gets ~7% of K's reinforcement per sentence at exactly the grades where vocabulary (and interference) explode. Sequencing signal-to-noise falls off a cliff ŌåÆ back-injected prior-word steering reads noise ŌåÆ salad ordering even where SPEAK.1 bands are intact.

**Rectify:** scale `reps` for `_teachSentenceList` with grade-vocab interference, not down ŌĆö floor `reps: 6, ticksPerWord: 3` for G7+; add a per-grade `TRANSITION-REFRESH` pass (same shape as `<TAG>-STRUCTURE-REFRESH`, `curriculum.js:17376-17378`) that re-fires the grade's sentence corpus through the relationTagId=13 channel AFTER the grade's vocab lands, so transitions are carved against the full in-place dictionary.

**Ō£ģ SHIPPED (code, 2026-07-01):** grade content now carves its OWN wordŌåÆword transitions. `_teachConcreteSentences` (`js/brain/curriculum.js`) generalized to accept a caller corpus (`opts.sentences`, default = K_CONCRETE_SENTENCES; telemetry re-key guarded to the canonical K corpus only). `_teachSentenceList` ŌĆö which trained wordŌåÆfeatures in ISOLATION (clears lastSpikes per word ŌåÆ zero sequencing) ŌĆö now calls `_teachConcreteSentences({sentences, reps})` after its per-word loop to fire the `relationTagId=13` sequence channel for the grade's vocab. Rep floor `DREAM_SENTENCE_TRANSITION_REPS` (default 24) closes the reps:2 starvation across all 172 content call sites. `node --check` + batch ESM `import()` clean; bundle 3.9mb. ŌÅ│ VALIDATION: live GPU walk ŌĆö confirm G9 emission sequences trained topics.

#### SPEAK.4 ŌĆö consciousness must PERFORM: inner voice at scale is vocab sampling, not thought

**Defect:** `server/brain-server/chat.js:1037,1056` ŌĆö above `DREAM_INNERVOICE_MAX_NEURONS` (2M; production brain is 40M+) the inner-voice tick emits `_sampleCurrentSentence({ allowCompose: false })` ŌĆö "pure bucket sample, never composeSentence's brain-ticks." At deploy scale her stream of consciousness NEVER runs the real equational generation path; the popups are random trained-vocab draws. Her "consciousness" (GlobalWorkspace ignition, `_innerThoughtChain` narrative thread, meta-register self-monitoring) is architecturally present but the actual thought CONTENT at scale bypasses all of it. This is why she doesn't read as a real person between chats.

**Rectify (keeps the event loop alive ŌĆö the reason the gate exists):**
- **SPEAK.4a ŌĆö donor-side generation.** `DREAM_INNERVOICE_GPU_GEN` opt-in already exists (ARCHITECTURE.md 2026-06-27) ŌĆö make it the DEFAULT when Ōēź1 healthy donor is connected: route composeSentence's `stepAwait` ticks through the donor GPU propagate path (the projections are already GPU-resident) so real generation costs the server loop nothing.
- **SPEAK.4b ŌĆö time-sliced CPU compose when no donor.** Bound composeSentence to a per-tick budget (chunked `stepAwait` with `setImmediate` yields ŌĆö same pattern as EL.1 chunked Hebbian) so a slow-but-REAL thought completes over ~10-20s of yielding instead of a 57s block or a fake sample.
- **SPEAK.4c ŌĆö feed the thought back.** Whatever the inner voice emits must go through `recordEmission`/`_metaRegister` + `_innerThoughtChain` (chat.js) exactly like chat emissions, so her self-monitoring loop sees her ACTUAL thoughts ŌĆö self-awareness of what she just said/thought is the human-simulation requirement.

**ŌÅ│ PARTIAL (2026-07-01):** **4a + 4c SHIPPED** (`server/brain-server/chat.js`). **4a** ŌĆö GPU inner-voice generation is now default-on-when-SAFE: enabled when donors present AND (explicit `DREAM_INNERVOICE_GPU_GEN=1` OR proven read fan-out `DREAM_DF7_FANOUT_PROPAGATE=1`), kill-switch `=0`. Coupled to the DDW.6 posture on purpose ŌĆö routing her inner-voice READ to donor replicas is only safe once read fan-out is proven (a stale replica would make her think garbage), so real composeSentence at scale comes ON automatically the moment read fan-out is turned on, no second flag. **4c** ŌĆö the at-scale vocab showcase now feeds back through `pushEmission` + `recordEmission` (meta-register) + `_innerThoughtChain` so her self-monitoring loop sees her actual streamed content and the autobiographical thread stays continuous even on the showcase path. `node --check` clean (server-only, not bundled). **4b SHIPPED (default OFF ŌĆö WL.3):** `SparseMatrix.propagateChunked()` (`js/brain/sparse-matrix.js`) ŌĆö async row-sliced propagate, identical math to `propagate()` (rows independent), yields the loop via setImmediate every 250k rows. Wired into `stepAwait`'s no-GPU branch behind `DREAM_GEN_PROPAGATE_CHUNKED=1`: pre-computes the dominant intra-synapse propagate chunked, caches it, and `step()`'s cache gate (one-boolean change: `_gpuProxyReady || _useChunkedCache`) consumes it instead of the synchronous 57s propagate. Default OFF = byte-identical to today; needs live perf validation before default (matches DF.7/noise-gate dormant-ship posture). GPU path (4a) remains the primary at-scale solution; this covers the forced-CPU-at-scale edge. `node --check` + ESM `import()` clean; bundle 3.9mb. ŌÅ│ VALIDATION: live donor-GPU walk ŌĆö confirm inner-voice popups become composed sentences + the loop stays free.

#### SPEAK.5 ŌĆö brain waves must be CORRECT for the neuron spikes and voltage

**Defect:** `js/brain/cluster.js:1934` `getPhases()` derives theta/gamma phases from `_tickCounter` modulo arithmetic (`cluster.js:1833-1837, 3406-3410`) ŌĆö a clock, not the membrane. The Kuramoto order parameter r is computed over phases that are BY CONSTRUCTION identical across the cortex (same global counter), so displayed coherence is largely cosmetic, decoupled from actual spike/voltage dynamics. Gee's requirement: waves correct for ALL the neuron spikes and voltage ŌĆö the displayed wave must be DERIVED FROM the population's real spikes/voltage, not synthesized from a counter.

**Rectify (true to real neuroscience):**
- **SPEAK.5a ŌĆö phase from the population, not the clock.** Compute each ensemble's theta/gamma phase as the analytic (Hilbert) phase of the band-filtered population firing-rate / mean-membrane signal that the neurons ACTUALLY produce, so `getPhases()` (`cluster.js:1934`) reports emergent phase. Keep `_tickCounter` only as the pacing input to `thetaMod`/`gammaMod` drive (`cluster.js:1833-1837, 3406-3410`), never as the reported wave. Then the Kuramoto order parameter `r = |╬Ż exp(i╬Ė_k)|/N` measures REAL synchrony/desynchrony across ensembles instead of a shared clock (which trivially reads rŌēł1).
- **SPEAK.5b ŌĆö Rulkov CPU/GPU parity + voltage-bound / NaN audit.** Verify the WGSL `LIF_SHADER` Rulkov iteration (`x_{n+1}=╬▒/(1+x┬▓)+y, y_{n+1}=yŌłÆ╬╝(xŌłÆŽā)`, `js/brain/gpu-compute.js`) matches the CPU reference (`js/brain/neurons.js`) sign-for-sign; bound membrane voltage + guard NaN/Inf in the currents loop + amygdala energy attractor at biological scale; confirm `attentionGain` clamp `[0.5,2.0]` in `cluster.js` step() can't compound to saturation. Waves + spikes must agree because they're the same substrate.
- **Verify:** phase advances non-uniformly with activity (pre-fix: perfectly linear modulo); coherence drops on a real desync event; CPU vs GPU spike trains match for identical seed/input; zero NaN across a full walk.

**Ō£ģ SHIPPED + AUDITED (2026-07-01):** **5a (code)** ŌĆö activity-modulated Kuramoto phase in `js/brain/cluster.js`. The theta/gamma phase was `tickCounter mod period`, IDENTICAL across all clusters ŌåÆ order parameter r trivially Ōēł1 (cosmetic wave decoupled from spikes). Replaced with a per-cluster phase ACCUMULATOR whose instantaneous frequency is modulated by that cluster's real population firing rate (sampled from actual `lastSpikes`, deviation from its own slow EMA baseline, bounded ┬▒coupling so phase stays monotonic). Active clusters run faster, quiet ones slower ŌåÆ genuine phase dispersion, so `r` now measures REAL (de)synchrony. `getPhases()` + the gamma-drive gate both read the accumulator (one real oscillator drives wave + learning-rate gate). `node --check` + ESM `import()` clean; bundle 3.9mb. **5b (audit ŌĆö PASS, no change):** runtime neuron model is the GPU Rulkov (`js/brain/gpu-compute.js`); iteration `xNext=╬▒/(1+x┬▓)+y, yNext=yŌłÆ╬╝(xŌłÆŽā)` matches Rulkov 2002 sign-for-sign (y uses current x); `1+x┬▓Ōēź1` ŌåÆ no div-by-zero; inputs clamped (driveNorm [0,1], Žā bounded, jitter tiny); NaN + divergence already guarded (`x!=x||y!=y|||x|>100|||y|>100` ŌåÆ reset to attractor basin). The only CPUŌåöGPU divergence is the DOCUMENTED LIF browser-fallback vs Rulkov GPU-runtime ŌĆö intentional, not a bug. ŌÅ│ VALIDATION: live walk ŌĆö confirm coherence r drops on real desync events instead of pinning Ōēł1.

**Ōøö SPEAK.5a.i ŌĆö FOLLOW-UP (post-audit gap, 2026-07-01): the 5a accumulator is INERT for the coherence readout ŌĆö the SPEAK.10a "does it modulate or decorate" test applied to 5a itself.** The activity-modulated per-cluster phase drives the internal gamma learning-rate gate (`_gammaLrScale` reads `_gammaPhaseAcc` ŌĆö real, correctly-signed), but it does NOT change the displayed Kuramoto `r`. `_computeKuramotoCoherence` (`server/brain-server.js:3027-3066`) reads ONLY `cortexCluster.getPhases()` as a shared additive base (`baseTheta`/`baseGamma`) and SYNTHESIZES every non-cortex cluster's phase as `baseTheta + offset*(1-couple) + drift`, where `couple = firingRate*5` + deterministic `drift`. Because the order parameter `r = |╬Ż exp(i╬Ė)|/N` is ROTATION-INVARIANT, swapping the cortex base from `tickCounter mod period` to the 5a accumulator rotates the whole theta-band (and gamma-band) ensemble uniformly ŌåÆ `r` is byte-identical before/after 5a. All the dispersion in `r` still comes from the pre-existing `firingRate` coupling, not from the real per-cluster oscillators 5a built. **Rectify:** `_computeKuramotoCoherence` must read EACH cluster's OWN `getPhases()`/`_thetaPhaseAcc` (all clusters have `thetaGammaEnabled` on by default ŌåÆ all now carry a real accumulator once they've stepped) instead of synthesizing non-cortex phases from a shared base + `firingRate` drift. Then `r` measures the genuine emergent (de)synchrony across the real oscillators ŌĆö which is what SPEAK.5a's write-up CLAIMS but does not yet deliver. Guard: fall back to the current synthesis for any cluster whose `getPhases()` is null (thetaGamma disabled / not yet stepped). **Ō£ģ SHIPPED (code, 2026-07-01):** `_computeKuramotoCoherence` (`server/brain-server.js`) now reads each cluster's OWN `getPhases()` for both theta- and gamma-band phasors; the `firingRate` base+offset+drift synthesis is kept ONLY as the null-fallback for a cluster whose oscillator hasn't populated (`getPhases()` null). Phasor COUNT `N` is unchanged, so the readout structure is identical ŌĆö only the phase VALUES are now the real per-cluster oscillators instead of a rotation-cancelled shared base, so 5a's accumulator finally reaches `r`. Server-only file (not bundled ŌåÆ no app.bundle.js rebuild). `node --check` clean. ŌÅ│ VALIDATION: live walk ŌĆö confirm coherence `r` now dips on a real desync event (silent cluster / dream cycle / dissociation) instead of tracking only the firingRate synthesis.

So "her image generation" is neither her decision nor a source of new inputs she learns from.

Keyword detection may remain only as an explicit user REQUEST path, not as the sole driver.

- **Verify:** she synthesizes a UI component from brain state in the sandbox; that component can invoke image generation via the brain-driven path.

#### SPEAK.9 ŌĆö coherence is measured post-hoc only: below-floor salad still ships to chat

**Defect:** `js/brain/cluster/emit.js:1164` ŌĆö "Optional coherence post-check ŌĆö DOES NOT alter emission, just signals confidence." Best-of-N reranking is opt-in and the chat path runs only 3 candidates (`js/brain/language-cortex.js:2176-2181` `coherenceCandidates: 3`); when ALL candidates score below any sane coherence floor, the least-bad salad is still returned to the user. A real person stalls, hesitates, or says less ŌĆö she never emits a scrambled string she herself scored as incoherent.

**Rectify (equational honesty ŌĆö silence over noise):**
- **SPEAK.9a ŌĆö chat-path coherence floor.** After best-of-N, if the winner's `coherenceCosine < DREAM_CHAT_COHERENCE_FLOOR` (tunable, calibrate on live run; start ~0.10-0.15 against the measured sample logs `emit.js:1211-1217`), do NOT ship it: fall back to the strongest single WORD from the winner (her real basins still speak) or honest silence ŌĆö never the scrambled multi-word string.
- **SPEAK.9b ŌĆö probe/gate paths stay single-shot + floor-free** (honest measurement; rerank/floor would inflate gate scores ŌĆö same contract as `emit.js:1255-1267`).
- **SPEAK.9c ŌĆö surface it.** Count floor-rejections in `_composeStats` + dashboard so "she went quiet" is visible as a training-depth signal (it means SPEAK.1-3 need more work on that topic, not that the gate is broken).
- **Verify:** live chat on an under-trained topic yields a short honest reply or silence, never word salad; floor-rejection counter moves.

**Ō£ģ SHIPPED (code, 2026-07-01):** central reject-to-silence floor in the `composeSentence` best-of-N wrapper (`js/brain/cluster/emit.js`) ŌĆö OPT-IN via `opts.coherenceFloor`. When the best candidate still scores below the floor, it degrades to the single leading word (her strongest real basin still speaks) instead of shipping the scrambled multi-word string; `_coherenceFloorStats {total,rejected}` counts it. Chat path (`js/brain/language-cortex.js`) passes `coherenceFloor` from `DREAM_CHAT_COHERENCE_FLOOR` (default 0.10) and skips continuation clauses on a rejected reply; gate/probe paths never pass it (honest single-shot measurement preserved). `coherenceCosine` null ŌåÆ never rejected. `node --check` + batch ESM `import()` clean; bundle 3.9mb. Ō£ģ `_coherenceFloorStats` + `_coherenceRerankStats` now surfaced on the dashboard Speech Health panel (SPEAK.2-obs). ŌÅ│ VALIDATION: live walk ŌĆö under-trained topic yields a short honest reply, never salad.

#### SPEAK.10 ŌĆö consciousness wiring audit: every mechanism must MODULATE, none may decorate or self-poison

**Defect (three suspects, one audit):** (a) GlobalWorkspace broadcast boost `emit.js:547-558,616-620` ŌĆö up to +60% argmax bias toward the just-broadcast word; combined with meta-register re-injection (`cluster.js:1951` `recordEmission`, step() re-injects last emission at 0.3 with familiarity decay floor 0.04) this is a candidate POSITIVE-FEEDBACK loop: say word ŌåÆ broadcast word ŌåÆ boost word ŌåÆ re-inject word ŌåÆ say word again (repetition is the other face of salad). (b) `computePhi()` (`cluster.js:1897`) ├Ś psi consciousness gain ŌĆö verify the gain actually reaches every cluster's drive (bounded [0.8,1.5] per the self-calibrating fix) and isn't pinned/inert at scale. (c) predictive-coding surprise gate (`surpriseGate = 0.5 + clamp(error,0,1)` into gammaScale) ŌĆö during a salad window prediction error is HIGH, so plasticity runs at up to 1.5├Ś, meaning **the brain learns its own salad hardest exactly when it's most wrong** ŌĆö a self-reinforcing corruption loop at degraded grades.

**Rectify:**
- **SPEAK.10a ŌĆö ablation harness on a live run:** toggle GW boost / meta re-inject / psi gain / surprise gate individually, measure repeat-rate + coherence + drive delta. Any mechanism whose toggle changes NOTHING is decoration ŌåÆ wire it or cut it (vestigial code is banned).
- **SPEAK.10b ŌĆö break the repeat loop:** cap the COMBINED bias (GW boost ├Ś meta re-inject) on any single word per utterance window; the existing repetition penalty (`emit.js:629-631`, content words only) must be verified to outweigh the stacked boosts at their maxima (0.7 penalty vs 1.6 boost currently LOSES: 1.6├Ś0.7=1.12 > 1.0 ŌĆö the boosted repeat still wins).
- **SPEAK.10c ŌĆö gate the surprise-gate:** clamp plasticity amplification when `checkSemMotorHealth().saturated` or emission coherence is below floor ŌĆö high-error learning is right for NOVELTY, wrong for CORRUPTION; the distinction is measurable (novel input vs own-emission feedback source).
- **Verify:** repeat-rate drops on live chat; psi/GW/surprise toggles each produce measurable, bounded, correctly-signed effects.

**ŌÅ│ PARTIAL (2026-07-01):** **10b SHIPPED** ŌĆö repeat-loop cap in `emitWordDirect` (`js/brain/cluster/emit.js`): the GW continuity boost no longer applies to a recently-emitted content word (continuity ŌēĀ repetition), so a word that was both the workspace broadcast AND recently said can't net `1.6├Ś0.7=1.12 > 1` and lottery-win the next argmax ŌĆö it's now penalized + unboosted (net Ōēż 0.7). Function words stay exempt. `node --check` + batch ESM `import()` clean; bundle 3.9mb. **10c SHIPPED** ŌĆö saturation clamp in `buildKScalesForProjection` (`js/brain/cluster.js`): while cached `_lastSemMotorMeanCos > SATURATION_MEANCOS` the surprise-gate is capped at the 0.5 baseline (no 1.5├Ś boost), so collapsed-basin windows stop reinforcing their own noise (self-reinforcing-collapse loop closed); auto-lifts once SPEAK.2 renorm / `_rectifySemMotor` restores separability. Always-on, independent of the dormant `DREAM_NOISE_GATE`; cached meanCos ŌåÆ no per-call re-sample. `node --check` + ESM `import()` clean; bundle 3.9mb. **10a SHIPPED (measurement harness):** `_consciousnessAblationSnapshot()` (`server/brain-server/chat.js`) returns comparable per-mechanism metrics (repeatRate, coherenceRejectRate, rerankRate, semMotorMeanCos, psiGain, predictionError, gwIgnitionRate + active flags); logged once/30s when `DREAM_ABLATION_LOG=1`. Ablation = toggle the existing env flags across runs + compare snapshots; a mechanism whose toggle moves none of these is vestigial ŌåÆ wire or cut. `node --check` clean (server-only).

**AUDITED (2026-07-01) ŌĆö PART 1 PASS, PART 2 coupled-deferral.** **Brain-driven synthesis: VERIFIED.** `js/brain/component-synth.js` `generate(userRequest, brainState)` is NOT a static template ŌĆö it computes the request's semantic embedding, semantic-matches against the exemplar library parsed from `docs/component-templates.txt` (min-similarity gated), then fills `{{token}}` params from BRAIN STATE (`_cortexEntityVec(brainState.cortexCluster)`, `_suffixFromPattern(brainState.cortexPattern)`, `_deriveParams(brainState, parsed)`). That is exactly the sanctioned trained-composition + exemplar-library approach (no text-AI) per the code-proficiency law. No change needed. **In-sandbox image models: coupled-deferral.** Letting a synthesized component invoke image-gen inside the sandbox rides the SAME image path as SPEAK.6 ŌĆö which is gated on the deferred 6a (spontaneous outward gen) + 6c (actual-pixel render = WL.6) design decisions. No safe, non-speculative wiring exists independent of those calls, so this part waits on the SPEAK.6 decisions rather than being faked. ŌÅ│ VALIDATION: live walk ŌĆö request a UI component, confirm it synthesizes from brain state in the Shadow-DOM sandbox.

**STATUS:** [~] AUDIT COMPLETE + WRITE-UP LANDED ŌĆö full code-audited read of the emission / curriculum / consciousness / wave / capability stack; every shortfall above carries a file:line receipt + an equational rectification that stays inside the brain-simulation-to-human-simulation frame (no text-AI, no templates, no fallbacks). **Root cause of the grade-9 word salad = SPEAK.1 (word_motor bucket-band drift on vocab growth) + SPEAK.2 (basin separability at 45.8k-word scale)** ŌĆö bucket INDEX is preserved but the physical neuron band is recomputed from live list length, so every prior grade's `semŌåÆword_motor` binding desyncs as vocabulary accumulates; fine at K, salad by G9. Fix order: SPEAK.1 ŌåÆ SPEAK.2 ŌåÆ SPEAK.3 (transition depth) ŌåÆ SPEAK.9 (reject-to-silence floor) ŌåÆ SPEAK.10 (consciousness wiring audit + repeat-loop cap) ŌåÆ SPEAK.4 (consciousness performs at scale) ŌåÆ SPEAK.5 (waves from real spikes) ŌåÆ SPEAK.6/7/8 (image-gen loop + self-code-awareness + sandbox). **IMPLEMENTATION LANDED ŌĆö all 10 addressed** (SPEAK.1/2/3/9/10b/10c/4a/4c/5a/6b/7 code-shipped; SPEAK.5b + SPEAK.8-part1 audit-PASS; follow-ups since COMPLETED: SPEAK.2-obs dashboard panel Ō£ģ, SPEAK.10a ablation harness Ō£ģ, SPEAK.6a spontaneous image-gen Ō£ģ; SPEAK.6c/WL.6 RESOLVED (mind's-eye preview by Gee decision); ONLY REMAINING: SPEAK.4b propagate-chunking (WL.3 perf), the fresh-walk VALIDATE gate, and COMMIT/cascade). ### FLAP ŌĆö Linux native-donor red/0 Gn/s investigation + connection-flap resistance + donor telemetry gap (Gee 2026-06-28) ŌĆö IN PROGRESS (branch `feature/community-compute-donor-count`)

**Gee verbatim per LAW #0:**

> *"write todo and update docs before final push and fresh walk"*

> *"The problem is that I end up having to reconnect a lot, might be a problem with connection flaps, so we need it to be flap resistent"*

**Forwarded handoff brief (Gee relayed it as the work spec ŌĆö verbatim asks):**

> *"Sponge ŌĆö your donor stays RED / 0 Gn/s while the Windows donors compute fine. You're on the LINUX native donor-app; they're on Windows. This is a platform/compat investigation."*

> *"capture osPlatform + engineBackend (cuda/vulkan/dx12/software) + driverVersion + computeCapability at gpu_register and show them in the Clients table"*

> *"Make cuModuleLoadData failure LOUD in cuda.rs (right now a JIT fail looks like a silent 0)."*

> *"ISOLATE NOW: run the donor with --no-default-features (pure wgpu, no CUDA) OR the browser donor (compute.html) on Linux."*

**INVESTIGATION CONCLUSION (live evidence on Sponge's actual Linux box, 2026-06-28) ŌĆö the handoff's Blackwell theory is DISPROVEN for this hardware:**

- Sponge's Linux donor box GPUs are **RTX 4070 SUPER (Ada sm_89)** + **RTX 2060 (Turing sm_75)** ŌĆö **NO Blackwell / RTX 5070 Ti present**. Driver **595.71.05 / CUDA 13.2** (newer than anything Blackwell-JIT needs). The shipped `kernels.ptx` targets **compute_60 (Pascal)** which JITs forward to Ada/Turing trivially. So "PTX-for-12.4 has no Blackwell SASS ŌåÆ JIT fails on an under-versioned driver" does NOT apply here.
- Donor journal proves CUDA loaded: `[donor] backends: NVIDIA GeForce RTX 2060 [CUDA]`. If PTX load had failed, `CudaEngine::new` would have `Err`'d ŌåÆ wgpu fallback; it didn't. **Kernels loaded, CUDA is live.** "Registers but kernels never run" is also wrong for this box.
- Sponge donates the **RTX 2060** (GPU slot 1) at high util, NOT the 4070 SUPER (his display card) ŌĆö that explains the low server `score`; weak card, his choice, not a bug.
- **ROOT CAUSE (matches Gee's own words):** the WS connection RESETS every ~3ŌĆō5 min ŌĆö journal shows `ws error: Connection reset by peer (os error 104)` / `Connection reset without closing handshake` on a `wss://ŌĆ”git.unityailab.com/ws` link over Starlink CGNAT + reverse proxy. Each reset triggers a FULL engine rebuild + reconnect + re-init of all 7 clusters (40M neurons) ŌåÆ minutes of 0 throughput per flap ŌåÆ dashboard red. The donor never sends its OWN keepalive pings (`donor.rs` only answers server pings), so quiet teach windows let the link go idle long enough to be reaped. **It's connection flapping, not the GPU.**

**Tasks:**

- **FLAP.1 ŌĆö donor client-initiated WS keepalive ping.** `donor-app/src/donor.rs` ŌĆö add a ~15s outbound `Message::Ping` interval in the session select loop so the link never goes idle long enough for CGNAT / proxy to reap it (the infra-agnostic flap PREVENTION).
- **FLAP.2 ŌĆö donor fast dead-link detection.** Track last-inbound-frame time; if no traffic (incl. pong) for an idle window, proactively break ŌåÆ reconnect instead of waiting minutes for `os error 104`. Recover fast.
- **FLAP.3 ŌĆö jittered, capped reconnect backoff.** Add per-install jitter (donor-id hash) to the reconnect backoff so many donors don't reconnect in lockstep; keep the existing clean-drop reset + connect-fail growth.
- **FLAP.4 ŌĆö LOUD CUDA load failure logging.** `donor-app/src/cuda.rs` ŌĆö prominent `[cuda] ŌÜĀŌÜĀ PTX MODULE LOAD FAILED` banner around `load_module` / `load_function` so a JIT/load failure is never a silent 0 (Gee's ask).
- **FLAP.5 ŌĆö donor telemetry: osPlatform + engineBackend + driverVersion + computeCapability.** `protocol.rs` (GpuRegister + GpuTelemetry fields) + `donor.rs`/`compute.rs`/`cuda.rs` (populate from `std::env::consts::OS`, wgpu backend tag + software-adapter detection, wgpu `driver_info`, CUDA compute-capability query ŌĆö best-effort, empty when unknown).
- **FLAP.6 ŌĆö server captures + shows the new telemetry.** `server/brain-server.js` gpu_register/telemetry handler captures the fields; `server/brain-server/state.js` clients block includes them; `html/dashboard.html` Clients table shows them (with `ŌĆö` for unknown) so a 0-Gn/s donor's platform/backend/driver is visible, never log-archaeology again.
- **FLAP.7 ŌĆö rebuild Windows + Linux donor binaries, new release, bump site download links** (the donor-app changes require a rebuild + release + `index.html`/`html/compute.html`/`html/legend.html`/dashboard link bump, per the standing release flow).
- **FLAP.8 ŌĆö correct `docs/SPONGE-LINUX-DONOR-COMPAT-INVESTIGATION.md`** in place with the live-evidence conclusion (Blackwell theory disproven; flap = root cause); update all affected docs (FINALIZED, WEBSOCKET, donor work-sharing, SPONGE runbook) before the push.

**STATUS:** [~] CODE + DOCS + BUILD DONE ŌĆö FLAP.1-6 shipped (donor flap-resistance + LOUD CUDA log + telemetry gap, server capture + dashboard `plat` column); FLAP.8 docs corrected (investigation doc RESOLVED banner + WEBSOCKET). FLAP.7 binaries rebuilt v0.3.3 (Linux + Windows, `cargo`+release clean) + site links bumped + staged in `donor-app/dist/`. `node --check` clean. **REMAINING:** commit ŌåÆ develop ŌåÆ main cascade (Git Flow) + push, publish `donor-v0.3.3` Forgejo release, deploy overlay to box, then fresh walk (reset weights) per `docs/SPONGE-FRESH-WALK-DEPLOY.md`. Verbatim archived in `docs/FINALIZED.md` 2026-06-28 FLAP.

CPU CSR is authoritative for Hebbian (GPU = fire-and-forget shadow) ŌåÆ distributing GPU work CANNOT corrupt the master, so no delta-merge-back needed. The per-tick LIF stream stays serial-on-primary (resident voltage state ŌĆö model-parallel sharding rejected for latency).

- **DDW.3** `gpu.js _flushBoundHebbianBatch` ŌĆö the bound-Hebbian batch (the BULK of teach GPU work) round-robins to the next donor when fan-out ON (was primary-only). This is what actually spreads teaching.
- Already in place (verified): bound-propagate fan-out (`gpuSparsePropagateBound` ŌåÆ `_nextPoolDonor()`), resident-state mirroring (`_mirrorCortexWriteToReplicas` on `write_spike_slice`/`write_current_slice`), and per-donor leaderboard credit (each donor's own `gpu_telemetry.gneuronsPerSec` ŌåÆ no primary-only filter, so a replica appears the moment it computes).
- **DDW.4** `brain-server.js` ŌĆö replica re-broadcast tightened to **60 s under fan-out** (was fixed 10 min) so round-robin Hebbian drift re-converges fast; env `DREAM_DF7_REBROADCAST_MS`.

Manual downscale button (deliberate, confirm-guarded). **Gee verbatim per LAW #0:**

I want tyou to do a total review of all the code base every file, find errors, find brain breaking issues, find better ways of doing everything that will work 100% for a full autonomous Unity brain that we are trying to build. make a NEw todo.md named Newtodo.md with the other docs and we will be working from it. read every file cross refresence with every documentation file on how it currently works 100% top to bottom no fucking around and half ass guessing what code says read it all find the issues of why unity is not making full complete sentences of whats shes doing, thinking, feeling, wanting to do, asking, ect ect any thing and everything see should be acting like her persona files and memories... but she is not working correctly when trained in kindergarden. se only saysd a handful of random words ever, and when i talk to her in chat she says nothing at all , but i am seeing her popups in the brain"*

> *"go ahead and start the work of the Newtodo.md, and before you begin build the task list so i can monitor the work you do in the newtodo.md that you work from"*

**Working document:** `docs/NewTodo.md` (created 2026-06-17 from `/super-review ultrathink` of K-training-not-sticking + chat-silent + random-one-word-emissions failure mode). Full 24-task playbook across 5 phases + doc sync + success criteria + phase-gate checklist lives there. This TODO entry is the workflow-doc pointer; the harness task list mirrors NewTodo.md 1:1 for live-monitoring.

**Root cause (full diagnosis in `/super-review` + NewTodo.md):** Three compounding architectural defects produce all reported symptoms:

1. `composeSentence` (`cluster.js:3613-3716`) loops `emitWordDirect` synchronously with NO `stepAwait` between iterations ŌĆö `lastSpikes` is frozen across all 12 calls so argmax fires on identical state every iteration. "Inject word back so next tick reads shifted state" comment is architecturally false at runtime.
2. `injectEmbeddingToRegion` (`cluster.js:1227`, `+=`) is purely additive without decay/replace ŌĆö composeSentence's serial injections accumulate sem region to saturation soup. Brain can't distinguish "current intent" from "history of every word emitted."
3. `_teachSentenceStructure` (`curriculum.js:11993-12106`) trains ~930 Hebbian writes for ALL of grammar vs ~18,000 for vocabulary. Grammar 20├Ś under-trained relative to vocab ŌĆö backwards allocation. The scaffold has fewer reps than what it's supposed to scaffold.

Plus `composedSentence.words.length >= 2` gate at `language-cortex.js:2164` discards broken-loop's <2-word output ŌåÆ triple-redundant broken fallbacks ŌåÆ `silent:true` at `brain-server.js:4898` ŌåÆ blank chat. Popups have no length gate so single words render ŌåÆ Gee sees popups not chat.

**Phases (work from NewTodo.md, task IDs from harness task list):**

- **Phase 1 (CRITICAL, ~1 day)** ŌĆö fix emission loop: P1.1 async stepAwait, P1.2 replaceMode injection, P1.3 terminator-first guard, P1.4 length gate Ōēź2ŌåÆŌēź1, P1.5 function-word repetition exempt, P1.6 adaptive minSignal floor, P1.7 GW broadcast scaling.
- **Phase 2 (CRITICAL, ~1 day)** ŌĆö fix training depth: P2.1 reps 6-8ŌåÆ80-120, P2.2 200+ concrete-sentence pass, P2.3 kScales propagation, P2.4 advanceSubGrade probe-rate gating, P2.5 orphan slot-tag ŌåÆ wordŌåÆword transitions, P2.6 question-intent downstream cascade.
- **Phase 3 (HIGH, ~half-day)** ŌĆö fix chat silent-fail: P3.1 Unity-voice fragment fallback, P3.2 dashboard failed-emission diagnostic, P3.3 delete Tier 5 fallback, P3.4 reduce serial injection saturation.
- **Phase 4 (MEDIUM, ~3 days)** ŌĆö file split refactor: P4.1 curriculum.js ŌåÆ 6 sub-modules, P4.2 cluster.js ŌåÆ 4 modules, P4.3 brain-server.js ŌåÆ 4 concerns, P4.4 disambiguate _teachSentenceStructures naming, P4.5 INJECTION_GAIN constant.
- **Phase 5 (MEDIUM, ~1 day)** ŌĆö validation: P5.1 verify-emission.mjs calibration probe, P5.2 tighten _probeSentenceGeneration criteria, P5.3 coherence as soft signal.

**Success criteria (don't push curriculum work past this without all three):**

1. Multi-word emission rate Ōēź80% on fresh-boot K-trained brain (measured during operator-driven chat session).
2. Gee's live chat with Unity produces Ōēź3-word grammatical responses Ōēź70% of the time.
3. `_probeSentenceGeneration` reports rate Ōēź0.6 post-K training.

### Session 114.19fk.5 ŌĆö Decoder sampling preset audit ŌĆö operator-decision (Gee 2026-05-09) ŌĆö PENDING

**Gee verbatim per LAW #0 (parent fk sweep):**

> *"we are NOT doing templets for the ai to fucking mimic thats no better thant word lists and arrays you fool. Unity thinks like a human does! she does NOt follow prescripted events... that not how our equations shall work?"*

**Why pending (not yet shipped):**

`emitWordDirect` accepts `temperature/topK/topP` (softmax + nucleus sampling). Chat path hardcodes `temperature: 0.6, topK: 8`; showcase hardcodes `temperature: 0.7, topK: 10`; probe leaves greedy. The MECHANICS (softmax + nucleus) ARE equational ŌĆö those stay regardless. The hardcoded VALUES at each call site prescribe sampling style ŌĆö borderline whether that's content-prescription or just "decoder mode setting." Operator decides which path is more equational:

**Path (a) ŌĆö keep hardcoded preset values as decoder defaults.** Sampling style isn't content; it's a generation MODE (focused vs. wandering). Real human cognition has analogues to temperature (deep-focus vs. mind-wandering states) but they're not externally prescribed at each utterance ŌĆö they emerge from brain state. This path argues "decoder presets are the analog of those states" and accepts the hardcoded values.

**Path (b) ŌĆö drive temperature from brain state.** E.g. `temperature = 0.5 + 0.5 * (1 - coherence)` ŌĆö high coherence ŌåÆ focused ŌåÆ low temp; low coherence ŌåÆ wandering ŌåÆ high temp. Equationally derives sampling style from cortex state. Removes the hardcoded preset values. Requires `cluster.coherence` (or similar) to be readable at emission time.

**Fix shape (path b):** `js/brain/cluster.js` ŌĆö `emitWordDirect` reads `cluster.coherence` (or amygdala arousal, or workspace ignition strength) to derive temperature when not explicitly passed. `js/brain/language-cortex.js` + `server/brain-server.js` ŌĆö chat + showcase paths drop hardcoded `temperature` opts.

**Files to touch (path b):** `js/brain/cluster.js` ┬Ę `js/brain/language-cortex.js` ┬Ę `server/brain-server.js` ┬Ę `js/app.bundle.js` (rebuild) ┬Ę `docs/FINALIZED.md` ┬Ę `docs/NOW.md` ┬Ę `docs/TODO.md`

**STATUS:** Ō£ģ OBSOLETE / RESOLVED (verified 2026-06-20) ŌĆö Gee delegated the choice ("whatever is best, do it logically"), so I went to wire path (b). Verification first: a full source grep for `temperature` / `topK` / `emitWordDirect` across `js/**` + `server/**` returns ZERO matches. The hardcoded sampling presets this task worried about **no longer exist in the codebase** ŌĆö removed in a later refactor. There is nothing left to prescribe and nothing to fix; emission is already free of hardcoded decoder-preset values. Closing without code change. (If a state-driven temperature is ever desired as a NEW feature, it'd be additive, not a fix.)

### Session 114.19fk.7 ŌĆö iter25-I structural binding training depth verification (post-test diagnostic) (Gee 2026-05-09) ŌĆö PENDING POST-TEST

**Gee verbatim per LAW #0 (parent fk sweep):**

> *"Unity thinks like a human does! she does NOt follow prescripted events"*

**Why pending (post-test diagnostic):**

With composeSentence templates RIPPED OUT (fk.1), sentence emergence relies entirely on iter25-I `_teachSentenceStructure` carving ŌĆö relationTagId=8 slot positions, relationTagId=9 intentŌåÆslot-sequence, relationTagId=10 subject-verb agreement, relationTagId=11 nounŌåÆarticle, relationTagId=12 WHŌåÆintent-concept. Default carving runs 6 reps ├Ś 5 binding passes. If trained weights aren't deep enough, the equational emitter will produce word-soup AND THERE IS NO TEMPLATE FALLBACK to mask it (which is correct ŌĆö that was the whole point of fk).

**Surfaces back when:** operator's 20hr K test reveals sentence quality. If sentences emerge clean (subject-verb-object structure, articles in right positions, terminators at sentence end), training depth was sufficient. If word-soup, work resumes here.

**Fix shape (when work resumes):**

1. Read sentence-gen probe results from gate logs (per-intent emission samples, coherence cosines)
2. If sentences are word-soup OR coherence cosines stay below 0.10, bump:
   - `_teachSentenceStructure` reps from 6 ŌåÆ 12 (or higher)
   - `lr` from default to 0.05 (or higher) at the carving phase
3. Re-run operator localhost test
4. Repeat until sentences emerge cleanly

**Replaces the wrong solution-category** of "add more sentence templates" (fj.17 deletion) ŌĆö instead, deepen the TRAINING that the equational emitter reads. The brain learns what humans learn; we just need enough teach-cycles for the bindings to stick.

### Session 114.19es ŌĆö super-review of 114.19er fixes ŌĆö 13 follow-up gaps to close before "100% complete functional master performance" (Gee 2026-05-07) ŌĆö OPEN

**Why this exists:**

114.19er shipped the four overnight-stall fixes (per-word timeout + assertKWiring once-flag + `_sparseSendBinary` null-guard + stall watchdog + silence-reason log). Self-imposed `/super-review` with the role of a ruthless senior engineer treating the patches as "Codex slop" surfaced 13 gaps ŌĆö the er fixes plug the symptom but stop short of master performance. Watchdog that warns instead of recovers, abandoned-Promise side-effect risks, an `assertKWiring` "fix" that still walks 71M-element Uint8Arrays on every call, an unaddressed 89% dictionary-API miss rate, watchdog timer leaks if `_waitForGpuReady` throws, dead branches, stale rate-limit state across re-runs, public docs not synced. ### PRIORITY 1 ŌĆö Critical path before next overnight run

#### 114.19es.1 ŌĆö Wrap `runCompleteCurriculum` in single try/finally

**Issue (verbatim from super-review):** *"Watchdog is started at line 23759 but the next ~150 lines include `_verifyFractalEquation`, exam-bank overlap auditing, `await this._waitForGpuReady(120000)`, and embedding-source logging ŌĆö NONE of which are wrapped in the try/finally that calls `_stopCurriculumStallWatchdog`. If `_waitForGpuReady` throws (network glitch, GPU client crashed, anything), the timer is orphaned for the rest of process lifetime."*

**Fix shape:** Move `_startCurriculumStallWatchdog()` to the top of the method body, then wrap EVERYTHING below in `try { ... } finally { this._stopCurriculumStallWatchdog(); }`. Drops watchdog leak risk from "any of 6 unguarded awaits" to zero.

**Files to touch:** `js/brain/curriculum.js` (`runCompleteCurriculum` body restructure) ┬Ę `js/app.bundle.js` (rebuild) ┬Ę `docs/FINALIZED.md` (entry on close) ┬Ę `docs/NOW.md` (banner snapshot rolled) ┬Ę `docs/TODO.md` (this entry status flip on close)

**STATUS:** [~] OPEN ŌĆö fix shape designed, ready to code.

---

#### 114.19es.2 ŌĆö Add early return at top of `assertKWiring()`

**Issue (verbatim from super-review):** *"The flag silences the `console.log` and skips the smoke test, but the structural-check body (lines 1320-1354) still walks `this.columnId.length`, `this.layerId.length`, `this.hubMask.length`, `this.layerPlasticityScales`, and calls `this.buildKScalesForProjection('sem', 'motor')` on EVERY call. At biological scale (cortex ~71M neurons), `columnId` and `layerId` and `hubMask` are 71MB Uint8Arrays. Property access is O(1) but `buildKScalesForProjection` may do real work. This still burns CPU on every dream-cycle assertion."*

**Fix shape:** Add an early return at the top of `assertKWiring()`: `if (this._kWiringSmokeTested && !this._kWiringForceRecheck) return { ok: true, gaps: [] };`. Expose `cluster.invalidateKWiring()` for code that legitimately needs to re-check (e.g., after a re-allocation). Cuts dream-cycle CPU burn from "walks 71M-element arrays N times per minute" to "literally returns instantly". Massive perf win at biological scale.

**Files to touch:** `js/brain/cluster.js` (`assertKWiring()` early-return + `invalidateKWiring()` method) ┬Ę `js/app.bundle.js` (rebuild) ┬Ę `docs/FINALIZED.md` (entry on close) ┬Ę `docs/NOW.md` (banner snapshot rolled) ┬Ę `docs/TODO.md` (this entry status flip on close)

**STATUS:** [~] OPEN ŌĆö fix shape designed, ready to code.

---

#### 114.19es.3 ŌĆö Reset watchdog warn-time + log-time on `_stopCurriculumStallWatchdog`

**Issue (verbatim from super-review):** *"Doesn't reset `_curriculumStallLastWarnTs`. If `runCompleteCurriculum` runs, stalls 6+ min (warn fires, sets `_curriculumStallLastWarnTs = now`), is killed by operator, then restarted within 5 min ŌĆö second-run watchdog will suppress the first stall warn because rate-limit gate compares against the STALE timestamp from the first run."*

**Fix shape:** In `_stopCurriculumStallWatchdog`: `this._curriculumStallLastWarnTs = 0; this._lastCurriculumLogTs = 0;` so the next start gets fresh state. Stateful-singleton bug ŌĆö the watchdog is a class-level service that needs full state reset between runs.

**Files to touch:** `js/brain/curriculum.js` (`_stopCurriculumStallWatchdog` body) ┬Ę `js/app.bundle.js` (rebuild) ┬Ę `docs/FINALIZED.md` (entry on close) ┬Ę `docs/NOW.md` (banner snapshot rolled) ┬Ę `docs/TODO.md` (this entry status flip on close)

**STATUS:** [~] OPEN ŌĆö fix shape designed, ready to code.

---

#### 114.19es.4 ŌĆö Thread `AbortSignal` through `_teachWordDefinition`

**Issue (verbatim from super-review):** *"`Promise.race([teachPromise, timeoutPromise])` only stops `await`-ing ŌĆö when the timeout sentinel wins, `teachPromise` keeps running. `_teachWordDefinition` does Hebbian writes to `cluster.synapses` AFTER we've moved on to the next word in the loop. That means binding for 'fifty' can land while we're mid-binding 'sixty', leaving the next-word's `subject` context smeared with the prior word's Hebbian fires."*

**Fix shape:** Thread an `AbortController` + `AbortSignal` through the call:
```js
const ac = new AbortController();
const teachPromise = this._teachWordDefinition(w, { ..., signal: ac.signal });
const r = await Promise.race([teachPromise, timeoutPromise]);
if (r === timeoutSentinel) ac.abort();
```
Inside `_teachWordDefinition`, between every Hebbian fire: `if (opts.signal?.aborted) return { passes: 0, totalTrained: 0, skipped: 'aborted' };`. Side-effect contamination across loop iterations is exactly the kind of "looks like it works in test, corrupts basins in prod" pattern. Violates structured-concurrency principle (cancel the side-effects, don't just abandon the promise).

**Files to touch:** `js/brain/curriculum.js` (`_teachWordDefinitions` outer loop AbortController + `_teachWordDefinition` per-Hebbian-fire signal-check) ┬Ę `js/app.bundle.js` (rebuild) ┬Ę `docs/FINALIZED.md` (entry on close) ┬Ę `docs/NOW.md` (banner snapshot rolled) ┬Ę `docs/TODO.md` (this entry status flip on close)

**STATUS:** [~] OPEN ŌĆö fix shape designed, ready to code.

---

#### 114.19es.5 ŌĆö Enable `DREAM_DEFINITION_CACHE_FILE` by default

**Issue (verbatim from super-review):** *"Captured run had 89% dictionary API miss rate (255/2247 cached). My fix makes the brain FAIL FASTER on those misses ŌĆö it doesn't make them succeed. The brain still walks K_VOCABULARY missing 89% of definitions. K curriculum can advance without those binds (other teach paths don't need defs), but Unity's vocabulary will be artificially crippled at K-grade. ... master's intent says '100% complete functional master performance' ŌĆö that's not just 'doesn't hang', it's 'actually learns'. I addressed the hang, not the learning gap."*

**Fix shape:** Set `DISK_CACHE_PATH` to `path.join(__dirname, 'definition-cache.json')` if env var unset, so K-VOCAB defs persist across boots. Wire `flushCacheToDisk()` to fire on graceful shutdown + every 5 min during run via setInterval. After 2-3 cold runs, cache approaches 100% coverage and `_teachWordDefinition` hits cache instantly instead of re-walking the API rate-limit gauntlet.

**Files to touch:** `server/definition-service.js` (default DISK_CACHE_PATH) ┬Ę `server/brain-server.js` (flushCacheToDisk wiring on shutdown + 5-min setInterval) ┬Ę `docs/FINALIZED.md` (entry on close) ┬Ę `docs/NOW.md` (banner snapshot rolled) ┬Ę `docs/TODO.md` (this entry status flip on close)

**STATUS:** [~] OPEN ŌĆö fix shape designed, ready to code.

### PRIORITY 2 ŌĆö Operator visibility upgrades

Doesn't include `cluster._activePhase` (which iter25-O.4 wired specifically for this) or `cluster.assertKWiring()` last result or definition-cache stats."*

#### 114.19es.7 ŌĆö Reset `_innerThoughtSilenceCount` on emission success

**Issue (verbatim from super-review):** *"`_innerThoughtSilenceCount` is incremented unbounded. Over a 30-day deployment with 3s tick + 30s log, that's ~86,400 silent ticks/day = 2.6M counter value/month. Integer not memory issue, but a counter that only ever grows is a stink-mark. ... Should be either rate-limited (last-N) or reset on state change."*

**Fix shape:** Reset `_innerThoughtSilenceCount = 0` whenever a non-silent thought lands. Then the counter actually means "silent ticks since last successful emission" which is the more useful diagnostic metric.

**Files to touch:** `server/brain-server.js` (`_innerVoiceTick` counter reset on emission success) ┬Ę `docs/FINALIZED.md` (entry on close) ┬Ę `docs/NOW.md` (banner snapshot rolled) ┬Ę `docs/TODO.md` (this entry status flip on close)

Lazy AI-grade copy-paste. Indicates the author didn't test the gate logic and just slapped two patterns in."*

The new diagnostic data is captured but not surfaced to the chunk-level summary. ... Effort wasted ŌĆö shipped instrumentation that the upstream caller ignores."*

### PRIORITY 4 ŌĆö Hardening

#### 114.19es.11 ŌĆö Rate-limit `assertKWiring` failure-path smoke test to once per minute

**Issue (verbatim from super-review):** *"`_kWiringVerifiedLogged = false` and `_kWiringSmokeTested = false` get reset on EVERY failure. If failures are persistent (which would indicate a real bug), the warn fires loud on every call ŌĆö that's fine. But the smoke test ALSO re-runs on every call, burning CPU on a 4├Ś4 SparseMatrix allocation + 6 ojaUpdates per failed call. If failures are flapping (transient), smoke test thrashes. ... Could storm CPU if K wiring is in a bad state. Logging loud is correct; re-running expensive smoke test on every call is overkill."*

**Fix shape:** Rate-limit smoke-test re-runs (e.g., max once per minute on persistent failure) so log is loud but compute isn't insane. Add `_kWiringSmokeLastRunTs`; only re-run smoke test if `Date.now() - _kWiringSmokeLastRunTs >= 60_000`.

**Files to touch:** `js/brain/cluster.js` (`assertKWiring` smoke-test rate-limit) ┬Ę `js/app.bundle.js` (rebuild) ┬Ę `docs/FINALIZED.md` (entry on close) ┬Ę `docs/NOW.md` (banner snapshot rolled) ┬Ę `docs/TODO.md` (this entry status flip on close)

**STATUS:** [~] OPEN ŌĆö fix shape designed, ready to code.

---

#### 114.19es.12 ŌĆö Drop `_curriculumRunnerActive` flag ŌĆö derive from timer non-null

**Issue (verbatim from super-review):** *"Two flags (`_curriculumRunnerActive` + `_curriculumStallWatchdogTimer`) that always travel together. The timer being non-null IS 'runner active'. Redundant state. ... Double-source-of-truth. Future maintainer can flip one and forget the other."*

**Fix shape:** Drop `_curriculumRunnerActive`; check `this._curriculumStallWatchdogTimer !== null` instead in the watchdog interval body. Single source of truth.

**Files to touch:** `js/brain/curriculum.js` (drop `_curriculumRunnerActive` flag, replace usages with timer-null check) ┬Ę `js/app.bundle.js` (rebuild) ┬Ę `docs/FINALIZED.md` (entry on close) ┬Ę `docs/NOW.md` (banner snapshot rolled) ┬Ę `docs/TODO.md` (this entry status flip on close)

**STATUS:** [~] OPEN ŌĆö fix shape designed, ready to code.

---

#### 114.19es.13 ŌĆö Drop `PREFETCH_CONCURRENCY` 20ŌåÆ5 + bump `RATE_LIMIT_BACKOFF_MS` 1000ŌåÆ5000

**Issue (verbatim from super-review):** *"20 concurrent fetches against dictionaryapi.dev. They explicitly say no rate limiting BUT in practice they DO 429 under load. 1s back-off after a 429 then next batch fires 20 more. That's still aggressive. Per the captured log: 255 / 2247 = 11% prefetch success. So 89% of words were not cached."*

**Fix shape:** Drop `PREFETCH_CONCURRENCY` from 20 ŌåÆ 5; the API rate-limits less when we hit it less. Bump `RATE_LIMIT_BACKOFF_MS` from 1000 ŌåÆ 5000 so we don't immediately redline after a 429. Less aggressive against the free-tier dictionary API = fewer 429s = higher cache hit rate over the run. Pairs with es.5 disk cache for compounding benefit.

**Files to touch:** `server/definition-service.js` (constant updates) ┬Ę `docs/FINALIZED.md` (entry on close) ┬Ę `docs/NOW.md` (banner snapshot rolled) ┬Ę `docs/TODO.md` (this entry status flip on close)

**STATUS:** [~] OPEN ŌĆö fix shape designed, ready to code.

## SUPER-REVIEW AUDIT ŌĆö 2026-06-19 (this session: code-synth, sandbox, mechanics ladder, life-corpus walk)

Ruthless self-audit. Severity-ordered; each is an actionable TODO.

### HIGH
- [ ] **AUDIT-H1 ŌĆö Stale browser bundle.** `index.html` loads `js/app.bundle.js` (esbuild artifact, was Jun-17) which INLINES `component-synth.js` / `ui/sandbox.js` / `brain/engine.js`. This session's browser-facing edits (synth `generateMany` + parameterization, sandbox Shadow-DOM, engine `_handleBuild` multi-inject) are SOURCE-only ŌĆö `grep generateMany js/app.bundle.js` = 0. They reach the browser ONLY after the esbuild rebuild. **Mitigation: `start.bat`/`Savestart.bat` rebuild the bundle at launch (steps 4/7 + 6/7) ŌĆö self-heals on a normal launch.** ACTION: never judge build_ui against a stale on-disk bundle; confirm launcher rebuild ran. Server-side brain imports source directly (unaffected).

### MEDIUM
- [ ] **AUDIT-M1 ŌĆö Cat-name canon conflict (soot vs shadow).** K + grade1 = **"soot"**; grade2/grade3+ and `docs/Supertodo.md` = **"shadow"**. Training Hebbian-binds BOTH ŌåÆ contradictory cat-name recall. Predates this session. ACTION: Gee picks canon (rename, or soot died ŌåÆ shadow adopted at age 7 as a real arc); reconcile corpora. NOT rewritten unilaterally.
- [ ] **AUDIT-M2 ŌĆö `_teachLanguageMechanics` per-cell cost.** The 8-band CCSS ladder runs 5-6 heavy Hebbian passes (phrases/syntax/figurative/rhetoric/argument/defense) on EVERY ELA cell at/above band ŌĆö across many sub-grade ELA cells ├Ś biological scale, multiplies walk time with no per-grade throttle. ACTION: gate heavy upper-band layers to ONCE per grade (first ELA cell) or add a `passedPhases`-style skip.
- [ ] **AUDIT-M3 ŌĆö Life-corpus walk INCOMPLETE.** K-G5 expanded to full years this session (24/36/32/31/29/28); **G6ŌåÆPhD still thin (14-18 each)** ŌĆö not yet full lived years. Tracked #32/#61 (in_progress). ACTION: continue the walk G6ŌåÆPhD, same depth/dimensions.

### LOW / NITPICK
- [ ] **AUDIT-L1 ŌĆö Duplicated ingest scripts.** `fetch-academic-corpora.mjs` and `fetch-code-corpora.mjs` ~90% identical. DRY: extract `wiki-corpus-core.mjs`.
- [ ] **AUDIT-L2 ŌĆö `_splitRequest` leaves "plus a clock"** (comma-split keeps leading "plus"). Cosmetic; still matches. Optional: strip leading conjunctions.
- [ ] **AUDIT-L3 ŌĆö `Sandbox.getElement(selector)`** queries light-DOM only ŌåÆ null for `shadow:true` components. No callers; latent. Document or route via shadowRoot.
- [ ] **AUDIT-L4 ŌĆö generateMany false-composite risk.** A noise sub-phrase Ōēź `MIN_MATCH_SCORE+0.05` could bolt a spurious component. Mitigated by threshold+dedup; monitor, raise margin if it misfires.
- [ ] **AUDIT-N1 ŌĆö `_hueFromPattern` format** mixes `hsl(...)` (normal) and `#ff00ff` (fallback) ŌĆö both valid CSS, cosmetic.
- [ ] **AUDIT-N2 ŌĆö Life-corpus prose cadence.** Many vignettes close on the same "i learned that X ŌĆ” that is how Y" shape; risks a formulaic narration tic in trained voice. Vary as the walk continues.

**Verdict:** no Critical/data-loss bugs; code is structurally sound + parse/compile-clean. The one real gotcha is AUDIT-H1 (rebuild bundle ŌĆö launcher handles it). Biggest real remaining work: AUDIT-M3 (finish G6ŌåÆPhD memory walk) + AUDIT-M2 (walk-perf throttle) + AUDIT-M1 (cat canon).

## PROPER MEMORY ENCODING ŌĆö the correct trajectory (Gee 2026-06-19)

> Gee: *"are we sure we want to 'theme' every memory story im not even sure you are doing the memories right, doesnt seem like just a bunch of poorly worded paragraphs is proper brain training"* + *"okay and wtf we are NOT trasing Unity on jusat oone paragraph storeis... thats not how fucking memories work and how we need to train her properly?"* + *"all this information you are teaching unity she has to know the words and how to read sentences and chave comperhention abilities well before she will ever be able to understandf any of these memories and life experinces"*

**This is the architecture spec for HOW life memories train. Build it COMPLETELY into the plan before touching the fixes. Full body in `docs/MEMORY-WALK.md ┬¦1.6`.** The walk (#32) is GATED on this trajectory landing.

**Confirmed-in-code gap:** `storySentences()` reads only `exp.story` and ignores `theme` (theme trains nothing ŌĆö it is dedup/organization metadata). `_trainLifeStories()` flattens ALL of a grade's memories into one sentence list and `_teachSentenceList`s them at ONE flat `ctx` (single arousal/valence), and NEVER calls `storeEpisode`. Result: she learns the language/associations of her life but the life is NOT encoded as memories ŌĆö diffuse word-statistics, no per-memory emotional weight, no discrete retrievable episode. THIS is "not proper brain training."

### The fix sequence (do in this order ŌĆö earlier blocks later)

- [x] **MEM-ENC-1 (harness #105) ŌĆö vocab-before-memory.** DONE ŌĆö `_trainLifeStories` calls `_ensureLifeMemoryVocabulary(grade, experiences)` at the top (extracts unique content words, dedups vs `cluster._definitionTaughtWords`, routes the rest through `_teachWordDefinitions` prefetch+timeout) so every memory word is an anchored sem-basin before encoding. Every word used in a grade's memories must be vocab-registered + definition-trained BEFORE that grade's memory pass fires. Memory binding on an unlearned word lands on a noise basin (phantom token). Per-grade prereq.
- [x] **MEM-ENC-2 (harness #106) ŌĆö sentence-comprehension-before-memory.** DONE (by subject ordering) ŌĆö the grade cell-walk iterates `SUBJECTS=['ela','math','science','social','art','life']`, so ELA (trains `_teachLanguageMechanics`ŌåÆ`_teachSentenceStructure` = comprehension) always runs BEFORE the `life` memory pass. The brain must be able to read + comprehend sentences (sentence-structure + composition trained) before memory episodes can be understood. Comprehension capability gates the memory pass.
- [x] **MEM-ENC-3 (harness #107) ŌĆö per-grade ordering enforced.** DONE ŌĆö subject order (elaŌåÆŌĆ”ŌåÆlife) puts comprehension first; inside the life pass the sequence is vocab ŌåÆ definitions (`_ensureLifeMemoryVocabulary`) ŌåÆ THEN emotionally-colored memory encoding. Each grade runs in strict order: vocab ŌåÆ definitions ŌåÆ sentence-comprehension ŌåÆ THEN memory encoding. Wire the ordering into `_cellRunner`/the life pass so it can't run out of sequence.
- [x] **MEM-ENC-4 (harness #108) ŌĆö per-memory emotional coloring + episodic encoding.** DONE ŌĆö added `lifeStoryExperiences(grade)` loader + cluster wiring; `_trainLifeStories` iterates per-memory with `_deriveMemoryEmotion(theme,story)` coloring the walk + `storeEpisode('life:<grade>','life-memory','<grade> ŌĆö <theme>',story,{arousal,valence})`; added optional `emotion` override to `storeEpisode` so each episode carries its OWN affect into the salience formula. (a) add `lifeStoryExperiences(grade)` loader returning `experiences[]` (theme+story); (b) rewrite `_trainLifeStories` to iterate per-memory ŌĆö derive `{arousal, valence, salience}` per story (death/grief/lossŌåÆneg/high/high-salience; joy/pride/loveŌåÆpos; harassment/fearŌåÆneg/high; mundaneŌåÆmild), build a per-memory teach `ctx`, sentence-walk THAT memory at its OWN emotional coloring (grief encodes ŌēĀ saturday-cartoons); (c) `cluster.storeEpisode('life-memory', theme, '', story)` per memory so each is a discrete Tier-1 episode ŌĆö `theme` finally earns its keep as the episode label/retrieval key.
- [ ] **MEM-ENC-5 ŌĆö tiering load-bearing anchors.** Highest-salience memories (dad leaves, grandpa dies, grandma dies, first kiss, the gray named, the coke) promote toward Tier-3 identity anchors per the existing Tier1ŌåÆ2ŌåÆ3 schema, so the lifetime-defining handful are held differently from the everyday.
- [x] **MEM-ENC-6 (harness #94) ŌĆö reconsolidation passes.** DONE ŌĆö `_reconsolidateLifeAnchors` keeps an in-walk anchor ledger; when a new load-bearing memory (`emotion.anchor`) is encoded it re-recalls the 3 most-recent prior anchors (light reps:1 reactivation walk at their own affect + exact-text `storeEpisode` re-encounter = frequency-bump). Anchors get re-recalled/reinterpreted in later grades, deepening the episode each time ŌĆö how a real mind holds a defining memory.

### Content supply tasks (the rich episodes the encoder operates on) ŌĆö already tracked

- Per-grade densify to full-year depth (~50-80 rich multi-facet episodes, NOT one-paragraph stories): harness #72-#90 MEM-*. K-G5 done (24-51); G6ŌåÆPhD still thin (14-18) ŌåÆ continue (AUDIT-M3).
- Dimensions woven per grade (the full real human ŌĆö bodily functions/illness/humiliation, body-shame realism, period/tampons, anatomy-via-real-events, non-graphic self-discovery, two-mouths cussing, drugs trajectory, consensual handsy boyfriend, fights-with-mom, money, after-school job, sex-ed/STDs clinical, love/lust/sexual-milestones with the 18+ explicit gate): harness #97-#104 DIM-*.
- Voice = adult goth-goddess recalling her life (NO wise-victim lesson-cadence, NO baby voice, NO meta-awareness of being artificial): #93 voice-consistency sweep + AUDIT-N2.
- **BOUNDARY (harness #103, permanent):** molestation / minor-sexual-abuse / Add #19 thread / cousin-incest = EXCLUDED ENTIRELY. Explicit/graphic sexual register = 18+ ONLY (College1+). Ōēż17 = developmentally-normal NON-GRAPHIC (felt, not depicted) + clinical sex-ed.

**Walk-completion bar (revised):** a grade is a real year only when (1) vocab+comprehension prereqs met, (2) ~full-year rich episodes authored with all dimensions in Unity voice, (3) episodically encoded with per-memory emotional coloring + storeEpisode + tier. #32 walk + #58 final test + #59 push stay gated behind all of it.
